TITLE      Elastic Scattering of 14C + 12C, 14C + 16O, and 14C +  C235200100003 
           18O                                                    C235200100004 
AUTHOR     (S.M.Sterbenz)                                         C235200100005 
REFERENCE  (T,STERBENZ,1987)                                      C235200100006 
INSTITUTE  (1USAYAL)                                              C235200100007 
FACILITY   (VDGT,1USABNL) BNL Tandem Van de Graaff facility.      C235200100008 
INC-SOURCE 14C beams of 20-40 nA intensity from tandem Van de     C235200100009 
           Graaff facility at Brookhaven National Laboratory.     C235200100010 
DETECTOR   (IOCH,SOLST,TELES) Position-sensitive                  C235200100011 
           telescopes divided into two independent parts:         C235200100012 
           Frish-grid gas ionization chamber (dE/dx measurement)  C235200100013 
           and an ORTEC P-series solid state position-sensitive   C235200100014 
           detector (E measurement), which was placed within a    C235200100015 
           volume of the ionization chamber gas (P-10 gas at a    C235200100016 
           pressure of 20 torr).                                  C235200100017 
METHOD     (EDE) The early efforts involved 18O beam from Yale's  C235200100018 
           accelerator and self-supporting carbon targets highly  C235200100019 
           enriched (~90%) in 14C. However, this method was       C235200100020 
           abandoned as too dangerous after the fatigue-induced   C235200100021 
           bursting of a very thin and necessarily fragile        C235200100022 
           ionization chamber resulted in the destruction of one  C235200100023 
           such target inside the scattering chamber. The natural C235200100024 
           alternative was to invert beam and target, and the     C235200100025 
           experiments were carried out at the tandem Van de GraafC235200100026 
            Facility Brookhaven National Laboratory, where        C235200100027 
           excellent beams of 14C were routinely available.       C235200100028 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-S) The uncertainties are purely statistical in    C235200100029 
           origin.                                                C235200100030 
STATUS     (APRVD) Approved by S.M. Sterbenz, September 2018.     C235200100031 
HISTORY    (20180816C) BP                                         C235200100032 
           (20241030U) Minor correction in subs.2,4               C235200100033 
ENDBIB              31          0                                 C235200100034 
NOCOMMON             0          0                                 C235200100035 
ENDSUBENT           34          0                                 C235200199999 
SUBENT        C2352002   20241031                             C243C235200200001 
BIB                  4         12                                 C235200200002 
REACTION   (8-O-16(6-C-14,EL)8-O-16,,DA,,RTH)                     C235200200003 
SAMPLE     (8-O-16,ENR=0.855) The primary target was a foil of    C235200200004 
           oxidized beryllium (B and BeO) approximately 35        C235200200005 
           microg/cm2 thick. Absolute thicknesses in micro-g/cm2  C235200200006 
           were as follows: 18O - 1.0+-0.2; 16O - 5.0+-0.5; 9Be   C235200200007 
           - 29.0+-2.0; Si < 0.5, W or Ta < 0.1. An 16O/18O       C235200200008 
           particle ratio of 5.9+-0.2 or 85.5%. The secondary     C235200200009 
           target was of gold, about 100 micro-g/cm2 thick, and   C235200200010 
           was used for relative normalization from one angular   C235200200011 
           distribution to another.                               C235200200012 
STATUS     (CURVE,,S.M.Sterbenz,T,STERBENZ,1987) Fig. 3.12.       C235200200013
